1st Apr.,2019:<br />
 I was asked to train an AutoPilot model for Indian Railways at their GPT-based ChatBot.<br /> II)< br >
I got the opportunity as well but it wasn't clear if they would be able to provide me with any data or support due to security reasons.
 III ) :
As soon after my conversation ended, i received call from someone claiming that he is working on similar project and his company wants us meet. He said we can discuss about this further over coffee.
 IV )
